We would structure this with your client's home equity covering at least the 20% down payment (CAD $190,000 for a $950,000 property).

5.  **Information on Typical Utility Setup Services in Oakville:**

We can confirm the exact school assignments based on the precise address once a property is selected, but it's safe to assume it's in a desirable family-oriented area.

2.  **Key Family-Friendly Features**: This magnificent 200m² home offers several family-friendly features:
    *   **Spacious Living**: A large 200m² home provides ample space for a family, including 4 bedrooms, ensuring comfort and privacy for all members.
    *   **Outdoor Space**: The property includes a **private garden** and a **patio**, ideal for children to play, family gatherings, and outdoor relaxation.
    *   **Quiet Residential Setting**: Located in a "quiet residential marina setting," it offers a safe and peaceful environment away from heavy traffic, conducive to family life.
    *   **Direct Water Access**: For families who enjoy water activities, the direct water access and private boat mooring offer unique recreational opportunities.

3.  **Home Equity for Down Payment and Bridge Financing**: Yes, it is absolutely feasible for your client to cover the CAD $190,000 down payment using their current home equity. This is a common and effective strategy. **Bridge financing** is highly relevant in this scenario. It is a short-term loan that "bridges" the gap between the purchase of a new home and the sale of the client's current home. It allows them to use the equity from their existing property to fund the down payment on the new Waterfront Property without waiting for their current home to sell, ensuring they don't miss out on their desired new home.

4.  **Scope of the "Basic Legal Package"**: The "Basic Legal Package" for CAD $800.00 covers the essential legal services required for a standard property purchase. This typically includes:

This allows your client to use the equity from their current home for the down payment on the new Waterfront Property without having to wait for their existing home to sell. This typically involves handling the legal transfer of property ownership from seller to buyer, ensuring clear title, and managing the necessary paperwork for the transaction. This package is comprehensive for standard property transfer and registration.
